[]\n\n        let analysisPreferences = preferenceData.series_preferences\n        if (analysisPreferences.length > 0) {\n            this.plotIdx = [].concat(...analysisPreferences)\n        } else {\n            this.plotIdx = []\n        }\n\n        if ((<ComparisonPreferenceModel>preferenceData)?.base_series_preferences != null) {\n            let baseAnalysisPreferences = (<ComparisonPreferenceModel>preferenceData).base_series_preferences\n            if (baseAnalysisPreferences.length > 0) {\n                this.basePlotIdx = [].concat(...baseAnalysisPreferences)\n            } else {\n                this.basePlotIdx = []\n            }\n        }\n\n        this.chartType = preferenceData.chart_type\n        this.stepRange = preferenceData.step_range\n        this.focusSmoothed = preferenceData.focus_smoothed\n        this.smoothValue = preferenceData.smooth_value\n    }\n\n    public render() {\n        if (this.series.length + this.baseSeries.length > 0) {\n            this.elem.classList.remove('hide')\n            this.renderLineChart()\n            this.renderSparkLines()\n        } else {\n            this.elem.classList.add('hide')\n        }\n    }\n\n    private renderLineChart() {\n        if (this.lineChartContainer == null) {\n            return\n        }\n        this.lineChartContainer.innerHTML = ''\n        $(this.lineChartContainer, $ => {\n            if (this.title != null) {\n                $('span', '.title.text-secondary', this.title)\n            }\n            new LineChart({\n                series: this.series,\n                baseSeries: this.baseSeries,\n                width: this.width,\n                plotIndex: this.plotIdx,\n                basePlotIdx: this.basePlotIdx,\n                chartType: this.chartType != null ? getChartType(this.chartType) : 'linear',\n                isDivergent: true,\n                stepRange: this.stepRange,\n                focusSmoothed: this.focusSmoothed,\n                smoothValue: this.smoothValue\n            }).render($)\n        })\n    }\n\n    private renderSparkLines() {\n        if (this.sparkLinesContainer == null) {\n            return\n        }\n        this.sparkLinesContainer.innerHTML = ''\n        $(this.sparkLinesContainer, $ => {\n            new SparkLines({\n                series: this.series,\n                baseSeries: this.baseSeries,\n                plotIdx: this.plotIdx,\n                basePlotIdx: this.basePlotIdx,\n                width: this.width,\n                isDivergent: true,\n                onlySelected: true,\n                smoothValue: this.smoothValue,\n                isMouseMoveOpt: false\n            }).render($)\n        })\n    }\n}",

private isLoading: boolean\n    private resolvers: any[]\n    private rejectors: any[]\n\n    constructor() {\n        this.isLoading = false\n        this.resolvers = []\n        this.rejectors = completes.\n            load().then((res: T) => {\n                this.resolve(res)\n            }).catch((err) => {\n                this.reject(err)\n            })\n        }\n\n        return     this.margin = Math.floor(windowWidth / 64)\n        this.chartWidth = windowWidth - 2 * this.margin - this.axisSize\n        this.chartHeight = Math.round(Math.min(this.chartWidth, windowHeight) / this.currentSeries.concat(this.baseSeries)) {\n            if (!this.uniqueItems.has(s.name)) {\n                this.uniqueItems.set(s.name, idx++)\n            }\n        }\n\n        this.baseSeries = this.baseSeries.filter((_, i) => this.basePlotIndex[i] == 1)\n        this.currentSeries = this.currentSeries.filter((_, i) => this.currentPlotIndex[i] == 1)\n\n = this.currentSeries.map((s, i) => {\n            s.series = smoothSeries(s.series, smoothWindow[0][i])\n            return s\n        })\n        this.baseSeries = this.baseSeries.map((s, i) => {\n            s.series = smoothSeries(s.series, smoothWindow[1][i])\n            return s\n        })\n\n        this.baseSeries = trimSteps(this.baseSeries, opt.stepRange[0], opt.stepRange[1], smoothRange)\n        this.currentSeries = trimSteps(this.currentSeries, opt.stepRange[0], opt.stepRange[1], smoothRange)\n\n        const stepExtent = getExtent(this.baseSeries.concat(this.currentSeries).map(s => s.series), d => d.step, false, true)\n        this.xScale = getScale(stepExtent, this.chartWidth, false)\n\n        this.chartColors = new ChartColors({\n            nColors: this.uniqueItems.size,\n            secondNColors: this.uniqueItems.size,\n            isDivergent: opt.isDivergent})\n    }\n\n    chartId = `chart_${Math.round(Math.random() * 1e9)}`\n\n    changeScale() {\n        let plotSeries = this.baseSeries.concat(this.currentSeries).map(s => s.series)\n        if (plotSeries.length == 0) {\n            this.yScale = d3.scaleLinear()\n                .domain([0, 0])\n                .range([0, 0]);\n            return\n        }\n        if (this.chartType === 'log') {\n            this.yScale = getLogScale(getExtent(plotSeries, d => this.focusSmoothed ? d.smoothed : d.value, false, true), -this.chartHeight)\n        } else {\n            this.yScale = getScale(getExtent(plotSeries, d => this.focusSmoothed ? d.smoothed : d.value, false), -this.chartHeight)\n        }\n    }\n\n    onTouchStart = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onTouchMove = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onTouchEnd = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseDown = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseUp = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseMove = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n    updateCursorStep(clientX: number) {\n        let cursorStep: number = null\n\n        if (this.svgBoundingClientRect == null) {\n            return\n        }\n\n        if (clientX) {\n            if (clientX > this.svgBoundingClientRect.right) {\n                clientX = this.svgBoundingClientRect.right\n            }\n\n            let currentX = func(cursorStep)\n        }\n    }\n\n    renderStep(cursorStep: number) {\n        this.stepElement.textContent = `Step : ${formatStep(cursorStep)}`\n    }\n\n    render($: WeyaElementFunction) {\n        this.changeScale()\n\n        $('div.relative', $ => {\n            if (this.baseSeries.length + this.currentSeries.length == 0) {\n                $('div', '.chart-overlay', $ => {\n          "import d3 from \"../../../d3\"\nimport {WeyaElement, WeyaElementFunction} from '../../../../../lib/weya/weya'\nimport {FillOptions, PlotOptions} from '../types'\nimport {PointValue} from \"../../../models/run\"\nimport {getSelectedIdx, mapRange, smoothSeries} from \"../utils\"\n\nexport interface LinePlotOptions extends PlotOptions {\n    xScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    series: PointValue[]\n    isBase?: boolean\n    renderHorizontalLine?: boolean\n    smoothFocused?: boolean\n}\n\nexport class LinePlot {\n    series: PointValue[]\n    xScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    yScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    color: string\n    circleElem: WeyaElement\n    lineElem: WeyaElement\n    smoothedLine: d3.Line<PointValue>\n    unsmoothedLine: d3.Line<PointValue>\n    bisect: d3.Bisector<number, number>\n    isBase: boolean\n    renderHorizontalLine: boolean\n    smoothFocused: boolean\n\n    constructor(opt: LinePlotOptions) {\n        this.series = opt.series\n        this.xScale = opt.xScale\n        this.yScale = opt.yScale\n        this.color = opt.color\n        this.isBase = opt.isBase ?? false\n        this.renderHorizontalLine = opt.renderHorizontalLine ?? false\n        this.smoothFocused = opt.smoothFocused ?? false\n\n        this.bisect = d3.bisector(function (d: PointValue) {\n            return d.step\n        }).left\n\n        this.smoothedLine = d3.line()\n            .curve(d3.curveMonotoneX)\n            .x((d, i) => {\n                return this.xScale(d.step)\n            })\n            .y((d) => {\n                return this.yScale(d.smoothed)\n            })\n\n        this.unsmoothedLine = d3.line()\n            .curve(d3.curveMonotoneX)\n            .x((d, i) => {\n                return this.xScale(d.step)\n            })\n            .y((d) => {\n                return this.yScale(d.value)\n            })\n    }\n\n    render($: WeyaElementFunction) {\n        $('g', $ => {\n            $(`path.smoothed-line.dropshadow${this.isBase ? '.base': '.current'}`,\n                {\n                    fill: 'none',\n                    stroke: this.color,\n                    d: this.smoothedLine(this.series) as string,\n                    \"stroke-dasharray\": this.isBase ? \"3 1\": \"\"\n                })\n            if (!this.isBase) {\n                $('path.unsmoothed-line'+(this.smoothFocused ? '.smooth-focused': ''),\n                    {\n                        fill: 'none',\n                        stroke: this.color,\n                        d: this.unsmoothedLine(this.series) as string\n                    })\n            }\n            $('g', $ => {\n                this.circleElem = $('circle',\n                    {\n                        fill: this.color\n                    })\n            })\n            $('g', $ => {\n                this.lineElem = $('line',\n                    {\n                        stroke: this.color\n                    })\n            })\n        })\n    }\n\n    renderIndicators(cursorStep: number | null) {\n        this.renderCircle(cursorStep)\n        if (this.renderHorizontalLine) {\n            this.renderLine(cursorStep)\n        }\n    }\n\n    private renderCircle(cursorStep: number | null) {\n        if (cursorStep != null) {\n            let idx = getSelectedIdx(this.series, this.bisect, cursorStep)\n\n            if (idx == -1)\n                return\n\n            this.circleElem.setAttribute(\"cx\", `${this.xScale(this.series[idx].step)}`)\n            this.circleElem.setAttribute(\"cy\", `${this.yScale(this.series[idx].smoothed)}`)\n            this.circleElem.setAttribute(\"r\", `5`)\n        }\n    }\n\n    private renderLine(cursorStep: number | null) {\n        if (cursorStep != null) {\n            let idx = getSelectedIdx(this.series, this.bisect, cursorStep)\n\n            if (idx == -1) {\n                return\n            }\n\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"x1\", `${this.xScale(this.xScale.domain()[0])}`)\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"x2\", `${this.xScale(this.xScale.domain()[1])}`)\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"y1\", `${this.yScale(this.series[idx].smoothed).toFixed(2)}`)\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"y2\", `${this.yScale(this.series[idx].smoothed).toFixed(2)}`)\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"stroke-width\", `1`)\n            this.lineElem.setAttribute(\"opacity\", `0.5`)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\ninterface LineFillOptions extends FillOptions {\n    xScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    series: PointValue[]\n    chartId?: string\n}\n\nexport class LineFill {\n    series: PointValue[]\n    chartId: string\n    xScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    yScale: d3.ScaleLinear<number, number>\n    color: string\n    colorIdx: number\n    smoothedLine\n    fill: string\n    dFill: string\n\n    constructor(opt: LineFillOptions) {\n        this.series = opt.series\n        this.xScale = opt.xScale\n        this.yScale = opt.yScale\n        this.color = opt.color\n        this.colorIdx = opt.colorIdx\n        this.chartId = opt.chartId\n\n        this.smoothedLine = d3.line()\n            .curve(d3.curveMonotoneX)\n            .x((d, i) => {\n                return this.xScale(d.step)\n            })\n            .y((d) => {\n                return this.yScale(d.smoothed)\n            })\n\n        let d = this.smoothedLine(this.series) as string\n        this.dFill = `M${this.xScale(this.series[0].step)},0L` + d.substr(1) +\n            `L${this.xScale(this.series[this.series.length - 1].step)},0`\n\n        this.fill = this.chartId ? `url(#gradient-${this.colorIdx}-${this.chartId}` : this.filteredPlotIdx.push(i)\n                this.plot.push(this.series[i])\n            }\n        }\n        if (this.plotIdx.length > 0 && Math.max(...this.plotIdx) < 0) {\n            this.plot = [this.series[0]]\n            this.filteredPlotIdx = [0]\n        }\n\n        const stepExtent = opt.stepExtend ? opt.stepExtend : getExtent(this.series.map(s => s.series), d => d.step)\n }\n\n    onTouchStart = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onTouchMove = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onTouchEnd = (ev: TouchEvent) => {\n        if (ev.touches.length !== 1) return\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.touches[0].clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseDown = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseUp = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n    onMouseMove = (ev: MouseEvent) => {\n        this.updateCursorStep(ev.clientX)\n    }\n\n\n    updateCursorStep(clientX: number) {\n        if this.svgBoundingClientRect.left - this.margin)\n            if (currentX) {\n                cursorStep = currentX\n            }\n        }\n\n        this.renderStep(cursorStep)\n        for (let }\n    }\n\n    renderStep(cursorStep: Date) {\n        this.stepElement.textContent = `${formatDateTime(cursorStep)}`\n    }\n\n    render($: WeyaElementFunction) {\n        this.changeScale()\n\n -        "import d3 from \"../../d3\"\n\nimport {PointValue, Indicator, IndicatorModel} from \"../../models/run\"\nimport {OUTLIER_MARGIN} from \"./constants\"\n\nexport function getExtentWithoutOutliers(series: PointValue[], func: (d: PointValue) => number): [number, number] {\n    let values = series.map(func)\n    values.sort((a, b) => a - b)\n    if (values.length === 0) {\n        return [0, 0]\n    }\n    if (values.length < 10) {\n        return [values[0], values[values.length - 1]]\n    }\n    let extent = [0, values.length - 1]\n    let margin = Math.floor(values.length * OUTLIER_MARGIN)\n    let stdDev = d3.deviation(values.slice(margin, values.length - margin))\n    if (stdDev == null) {\n        stdDev = (values[values.length - margin - 1] - values[margin]) / 2\n    }\n    for (; extent[0] < margin; extent[0]++) {\n        if (values[extent[0]] + stdDev * 2 > values[margin]) {\n            break\n        }\n    }\n    for (; extent[1] > values.length - margin - 1; extent[1]--) {\n        if (values[extent[1]] - stdDev * 2 < values[values.length - margin - 1]) {\n            break\n        }\n    }\n\n    return [values[extent[0]], values[extent[1]]]\n}\n\nexport function getExtent(series: PointValue[][], func: (d: PointValue) => number, forceZero: boolean = false, skipZero: boolean = false): [number, number] {\n    if (series.length === 0) {\n        return [0, 0]\n    }\n\n    let extent = getExtentWithoutOutliers(series[0], func)\n\n    for (let s of series) {\n        let e = getExtentWithoutOutliers(s, func)\n\n        if (skipZero && e[0] === 0) {\n            continue\n        }\n\n        extent[0] = Math.min(e[0], extent[0])\n        extent[1] = Math.max(e[1], extent[1])\n    }\n\n    if (skipZero) {\n        return extent\n    }\n\n    if (forceZero || (extent[0] > 0 && extent[0] / extent[1] < 0.1)) {\n        extent[0] = Math.min(0, extent[0])\n    }\n\n    return extent\n}\n\nexport function getScale(extent: [number, number], size: number, isNice: boolean = true): d3.ScaleLinear<number, number> {\n    if (isNice) {\n        return d3.scaleLinear()\n            .domain(extent).nice()\n            .range([0, size])\n    } else {\n        return d3.scaleLinear()\n            .domain(extent)\n            .range([0, size])\n    }\n}\n\nexport function mapRange(value: number, fromSource: number, toSource: number, fromTarget: number, toTarget: number) {\n    return (value - fromSource) / (toSource - fromSource) * (toTarget - fromTarget) + fromTarget;\n}\n\nexport function getLogScale(extent: [number, number], size: number): d3.ScaleLogarithmic<number, number> {\n    return d3.scaleLog()\n        .domain(extent)\n        .range([0, size])\n}\n\nexport function getTimeScale(extent: [Date, Date], size: number): d3.ScaleTime<number, number> {\n    return d3.scaleTime()\n        .domain(extent)\n        .range([0, size])\n}\n\nexport function toDate(time: number) {\n    return new Date(time * 1000)\n}\n\nexport function smoothSeries(series: PointValue[], windowSize: number): PointValue[] {\n    let result: PointValue[] = []\n    windowSize = ~~windowSize\n    let extraWindow = windowSize / 2\n    extraWindow = ~~extraWindow\n    if (series.length <= windowSize) {\n        return series\n    }\n\n    let count = 0\n    let total = 0\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < series.length + extraWindow; i++) {\n        let j = i - extraWindow\n        if (i < series.length) {\n            total += series[i].value\n            count++\n        }\n        if (j - extraWindow - 1 >= 0) {\n            total -= series[j - extraWindow - 1].value\n            count--\n        }\n        if (j>=0) {\n            result.push({step: series[j].step, value: series[j].value, smoothed: total / count, lastStep: series[j].lastStep})\n        }\n    }\n    return result\n}\n\nexport function fillPlotPreferences(series: Indicator[], currentPlotIdx: number[] = []) {\n    if (currentPlotIdx.length != 0) {\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length == series.length) {\n            return currentPlotIdx\n        }\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length > series.length) {\n            return currentPlotIdx.slice(0, series.length)\n        }\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length < series.length) {\n            while (currentPlotIdx.length != series.length) {\n                currentPlotIdx.push(-1)\n            }\n            return currentPlotIdx\n        }\n    }\n\n    let plotIdx = []\n    for (let s of series) {\n        plotIdx.push(-1)\n    }\n\n    return plotIdx\n}\n\nexport function toPointValue(s: IndicatorModel) {\n    let res: PointValue[] = []\n    for (let i = 0; i < s.step.length; ++i) {\n        res.push({step: s.step[i], value: s.value[i], smoothed: s.value[i], lastStep: s.last_step[i]})\n    }\n\n    return res\n}\n\nexport function getSelectedIdx(series: any[], bisect: typeof d3.bisect, currentX?: any | null, stepKey: string = 'step') {\n    let idx = series.length - 1\n    if (currentX != null) {\n        idx = bisect(series, currentX)\n        if (idx < series.length) {\n            if (idx !== 0) {\n                idx = Math.abs(currentX - series[idx - 1][stepKey]) > Math.abs(currentX - series[idx][stepKey]) ?\n                    idx : idx - 1\n            }\n\n            return idx\n        } else {\n            return series.length - 1\n        }\n    }\n\n    return idx\n}\n\nexport function getChartType(index: number): 'log' | 'linear' {\n    return index === 0 ? 'linear' : 'log'\n}\n\nexport function trimSteps(series: Indicator[], min: number, max: number, smoothRange: number = 0) : Indicator[] {\n    smoothRange /= 2 // remove half from each end\n    return  <Indicator[]>series.map(s => {\n        let res = {...s}\n        res.series = []\n\n        if (s.series.length == 0) {\n            return res\n        }\n\n        let start = 1e9, end = -1\n        let localMin = min\n        let localMax = max\n\n        if (localMin == -1) {\n            localMin = s.series[0].step\n        }\n        localMin = Math.max(localMin, s.series[0].step + smoothRange)\n\n        if (localMax == -1) {\n            localMax = s.series[s.series.length - 1].step\n        }\n        localMax = Math.min(localMax, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - smoothRange)\n\n        for (let i = 0; i < s.series.length; i++) {\n            let p = s.series[i]\n            if ((p.step >= localMin || localMin == -1) && (p.step <= localMax || localMax == -1)) {\n                start = Math.min(start, i)\n                end = Math.max(end, i)\n                res.series.push(p)\n            }\n        }\n\n        return res\n    })\n}\n\nexport function trimStepsOfPoints(series: PointValue[][], min: number, max: number, smoothRange: number = 0) : PointValue[][] {\n     smoothRange /= 2 // remove half from each end\n    return series.map(s => {\n        let res = []\n        let start = 1e9, end = -1\n        let localMin = min\n        let localMax = max\n\n        if (localMin == -1) {\n            localMin = s[0].step\n        }\n        localMin = Math.max(localMin, s[0].step + smoothRange)\n\n        if (localMax == -1) {\n            localMax = s[s.length - 1].step\n        }\n        localMax = Math.min(localMax, s[s.length - 1].step - smoothRange)\n        for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {\n            let p = s[i]\n            if ((p.step >= localMin || localMin == -1) && (p.step <= localMax || localMax == -1)) {\n                start = Math.min(start, i)\n                end = Math.max(end, i)\n                res.push(p)\n            }\n        }\n\n        return res\n    })\n}\n\n/**\n * Calculates the smooth window size for each series in the current and base series.\n * The smooth window size is determined based on the minimum range of steps in the series and the provided smooth value.\n *\n * @param {Indicator[]} currentSeries - The current series of data.\n * @param {Indicator[]} baseSeries - The base series of data for comparison.\n * @param {number} smoothValue - The value to be used for smoothing the data.\n * @returns {[number[][], number]} - Returns an array of smooth window sizes for each series. and the smooth window size in steps.\n * (ret[0] = smooth window for current series, ret[1] = smooth window for base series\n */\nexport function getSmoothWindow(currentSeries: Indicator[], baseSeries: Indicator[], smoothValue: number): [number[][], number] {\n    let minRange: number = Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER\n    for (let s of currentSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length > 0 && !s.is_summary) {\n            minRange = Math.min(minRange, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - s.series[0].step)\n        }\n    }\n    for (let s of baseSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length > 0 && !s.is_summary) {\n            minRange = Math.min(minRange, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - s.series[0].step)\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (minRange == Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER) {\n        let stepRange = [[],[]]\n        for (let s of currentSeries) {\n            stepRange[0].push(1)\n        }\n        for (let s of baseSeries) {\n            stepRange[1].push(1)\n        }\n        return [stepRange, 0]\n    }\n\n    let smoothRange = mapRange(smoothValue, 1, 100, 1, minRange/10)\n\n    let stepRange = [[],[]]\n    for (let s of currentSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length >= 2 && !s.is_summary) {\n            let stepGap = s.series[1].step - s.series[0].step\n            let numSteps = Math.max(1, Math.floor(smoothRange / stepGap))\n            stepRange[0].push(numSteps)\n        } else {\n            stepRange[0].push(1)\n        }\n    }\n    for (let s of baseSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length >= 2 && !s.is_summary) {\n            let stepGap = s.series[1].step - s.series[0].step\n            let numSteps = Math.max(1, Math.floor(smoothRange / stepGap))\n            stepRange[1].push(numSteps)\n        } else {\n            stepRange[1].push(1)\n        }\n    }\n\n    return [stepRange, smoothRange]\n}\n\n// Default smoothing function from backend\nfunction meanAngle(smoothed: PointValue[], aspectRatio: number) {\n    let xRange = smoothed[smoothed.length - 1].lastStep - smoothed[0].lastStep\n    let yExtent = getExtent([smoothed], d => d.smoothed)\n    let yRange = yExtent[1] - yExtent[0]\n\n    if (xRange < 1e-9 || yRange < 1e-9) {\n        return 0\n    }\n\n    let angles = []\n    for (let i = 1; i < smoothed.length; i++) {\n        let dx = (smoothed[i].lastStep - smoothed[i - 1].lastStep) / xRange\n        let dy = (smoothed[i].smoothed - smoothed[i - 1].smoothed) / yRange\n        angles.push(Math.atan2(Math.abs(dy) * aspectRatio, Math.abs(dx)))\n    }\n\n    let angleSum = 0\n    for (let a of angles) {\n        angleSum += a\n    }\n    return angleSum / angles.length\n}\n\nexport function smooth45(series: PointValue[]): PointValue[] {\n    const MIN_SMOOTH_POINTS = 1\n    let fortyFive = Math.PI / 4\n    let hi = Math.max(1, series.length / MIN_SMOOTH_POINTS)\n    let lo = 1\n\n    let smoothed = smoothSeries(series, hi)\n\n    while (lo < hi) {\n        let m = (lo + hi) / 2\n        smoothed = smoothSeries(series, m)\n        let angle = meanAngle(smoothed, 0.5)\n        if (angle > fortyFive) {\n            lo = m + 1\n        } else {\n            hi = m\n        }\n    }\n\n    return smoothSeries(series, hi)\n}",
+        "import d3 from \"../../d3\"\n\nimport {Indicator, IndicatorModel, PointValue} from \"../../models/run\"\nimport {OUTLIER_MARGIN} from \"./constants\"\n\nexport function getExtentWithoutOutliers(series: PointValue[], func: (d: PointValue) => number): [number, number] {\n    let values = series.map(func)\n    values.sort((a, b) => a - b)\n    if (values.length === 0) {\n        return [0, 0]\n    }\n    if (values.length < 10) {\n        return [values[0], values[values.length - 1]]\n    }\n    let extent = [0, values.length - 1]\n    let margin = Math.floor(values.length * OUTLIER_MARGIN)\n    let stdDev = d3.deviation(values.slice(margin, values.length - margin))\n    if (stdDev == null) {\n        stdDev = (values[values.length - margin - 1] - values[margin]) / 2\n    }\n    for (; extent[0] < margin; extent[0]++) {\n        if (values[extent[0]] + stdDev * 2 > values[margin]) {\n            break\n        }\n    }\n    for (; extent[1] > values.length - margin - 1; extent[1]--) {\n        if (values[extent[1]] - stdDev * 2 < values[values.length - margin - 1]) {\n            break\n        }\n    }\n\n    return [values[extent[0]], values[extent[1]]]\n}\n\nexport function getExtent(series: PointValue[][], func: (d: PointValue) => number, forceZero: boolean = false, skipZero: boolean = false): [number, number] {\n    if (series.length === 0) {\n        return [0, 0]\n    }\n\n    let extent = getExtentWithoutOutliers(series[0], func)\n\n    for (let s of series) {\n        let e = getExtentWithoutOutliers(s, func)\n\n        if (skipZero && e[0] === 0) {\n            continue\n        }\n\n        extent[0] = Math.min(e[0], extent[0])\n        extent[1] = Math.max(e[1], extent[1])\n    }\n\n    if (skipZero) {\n        return extent\n    }\n\n    if (forceZero || (extent[0] > 0 && extent[0] / extent[1] < 0.1)) {\n        extent[0] = Math.min(0, extent[0])\n    }\n\n    return extent\n}\n\nexport function getScale(extent: [number, number], size: number, isNice: boolean = true): d3.ScaleLinear<number, number> {\n    if (isNice) {\n        return d3.scaleLinear()\n            .domain(extent).nice()\n            .range([0, size])\n    } else {\n        return d3.scaleLinear()\n            .domain(extent)\n            .range([0, size])\n    }\n}\n\nexport function mapRange(value: number, fromSource: number, toSource: number, fromTarget: number, toTarget: number) {\n    return (value - fromSource) / (toSource - fromSource) * (toTarget - fromTarget) + fromTarget;\n}\n\nexport function getLogScale(extent: [number, number], size: number): d3.ScaleLogarithmic<number, number> {\n    return d3.scaleLog()\n        .domain(extent)\n        .range([0, size])\n}\n\nexport function getTimeScale(extent: [Date, Date], size: number): d3.ScaleTime<number, number> {\n    return d3.scaleTime()\n        .domain(extent)\n        .range([0, size])\n}\n\nexport function toDate(time: number) {\n    return new Date(time * 1000)\n}\n\nexport function smoothSeries(series: PointValue[], windowSize: number): PointValue[] {\n    let result: PointValue[] = []\n    windowSize = ~~windowSize\n    let extraWindow = windowSize / 2\n    extraWindow = ~~extraWindow\n    if (series.length <= windowSize) {\n        return series\n    }\n\n    let count = 0\n    let total = 0\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < series.length + extraWindow; i++) {\n        let j = i - extraWindow\n        if (i < series.length) {\n            total += series[i].value\n            count++\n        }\n        if (j - extraWindow - 1 >= 0) {\n            total -= series[j - extraWindow - 1].value\n            count--\n        }\n        if (j>=0) {\n            result.push({step: series[j].step, value: series[j].value, smoothed: total / count, lastStep: series[j].lastStep})\n        }\n    }\n    return result\n}\n\nexport function fillPlotPreferences(series: Indicator[], currentPlotIdx: number[] = []) {\n    if (currentPlotIdx.length != 0) {\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length == series.length) {\n            return currentPlotIdx\n        }\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length > series.length) {\n            return currentPlotIdx.slice(0, series.length)\n        }\n        if (currentPlotIdx.length < series.length) {\n            while (currentPlotIdx.length != series.length) {\n                currentPlotIdx.push(-1)\n            }\n            return currentPlotIdx\n        }\n    }\n\n    let plotIdx = []\n    for (let s of series) {\n        plotIdx.push(-1)\n    }\n\n    return plotIdx\n}\n\nexport function toPointValue(s: IndicatorModel) {\n    let res: PointValue[] = []\n    let step = getListFromBinary(s.step)\n    let value = getListFromBinary(s.value)\n    let lastStep = getListFromBinary(s.last_step)\n    for (let i = 0; i < step.length; ++i) {\n        res.push({step: step[i], value: value[i], smoothed: value[i], lastStep: lastStep[i]})\n    }\n\n    return res\n}\n\nexport function getSelectedIdx(series: any[], bisect: typeof d3.bisect, currentX?: any | null, stepKey: string = 'step') {\n    let idx = series.length - 1\n    if (currentX != null) {\n        idx = bisect(series, currentX)\n        if (idx < series.length) {\n            if (idx !== 0) {\n                idx = Math.abs(currentX - series[idx - 1][stepKey]) > Math.abs(currentX - series[idx][stepKey]) ?\n                    idx : idx - 1\n            }\n\n            return idx\n        } else {\n            return series.length - 1\n        }\n    }\n\n    return idx\n}\n\nexport function getChartType(index: number): 'log' | 'linear' {\n    return index === 0 ? 'linear' : 'log'\n}\n\nexport function trimSteps(series: Indicator[], min: number, max: number, smoothRange: number = 0) : Indicator[] {\n    smoothRange /= 2 // remove half from each end\n    return  <Indicator[]>series.map(s => {\n        let res = {...s}\n        res.series = []\n\n        if (s.series.length == 0) {\n            return res\n        }\n\n        let start = 1e9, end = -1\n        let localMin = min\n        let localMax = max\n\n        if (localMin == -1) {\n            localMin = s.series[0].step\n        }\n        localMin = Math.max(localMin, s.series[0].step + smoothRange)\n\n        if (localMax == -1) {\n            localMax = s.series[s.series.length - 1].step\n        }\n        localMax = Math.min(localMax, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - smoothRange)\n\n        for (let i = 0; i < s.series.length; i++) {\n            let p = s.series[i]\n            if ((p.step >= localMin || localMin == -1) && (p.step <= localMax || localMax == -1)) {\n                start = Math.min(start, i)\n                end = Math.max(end, i)\n                res.series.push(p)\n            }\n        }\n\n        return res\n    })\n}\n\nexport function trimStepsOfPoints(series: PointValue[][], min: number, max: number, smoothRange: number = 0) : PointValue[][] {\n     smoothRange /= 2 // remove half from each end\n    return series.map(s => {\n        let res = []\n        let start = 1e9, end = -1\n        let localMin = min\n        let localMax = max\n\n        if (localMin == -1) {\n            localMin = s[0].step\n        }\n        localMin = Math.max(localMin, s[0].step + smoothRange)\n\n        if (localMax == -1) {\n            localMax = s[s.length - The current series of data.\n * @param {Indicator[]} baseSeries - The base series of data for comparison.\n * @param {number} smoothValue - The value to be used for smoothing the data.\n * @returns {[number[][], number]} - Returns an array of smooth window sizes for each series. and the smooth window size in steps.\n * (ret[0] = smooth window for current series, ret[1] = smooth window for base series\n */\nexport function getSmoothWindow(currentSeries: Indicator[], baseSeries: Indicator[], smoothValue: number): [number[][], number] {\n    let minRange: number = Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER\n    for (let s of currentSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length > 0 && !s.is_summary) {\n            minRange = Math.min(minRange, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - s.series[0].step)\n        }\n    }\n    for (let s of baseSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length > 0 && !s.is_summary) {\n            minRange = Math.min(minRange, s.series[s.series.length - 1].step - s.series[0].step)\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (minRange == Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER) {\n        let stepRange = [[],[]]\n        for (let s of currentSeries) {\n            stepRange[0].push(1)\n        }\n        for (let s of baseSeries) {\n            stepRange[1].push(1)\n        }\n        return [stepRange, 0]\n    }\n\n    let smoothRange = mapRange(smoothValue, 1, 100, 1, minRange/10)\n\n    let stepRange = [[],[]]\n    for (let s of currentSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length >= 2 && !s.is_summary) {\n            let stepGap = s.series[1].step - s.series[0].step\n            let numSteps = Math.max(1, Math.floor(smoothRange / stepGap))\n            stepRange[0].push(numSteps)\n        } else {\n            stepRange[0].push(1)\n        }\n    }\n    for (let s of baseSeries) {\n        if (s.series.length >= 2 && !s.is_summary) {\n            let stepGap = s.series[1].step - s.series[0].step\n            let numSteps = Math.max(1, Math.floor(smoothRange / stepGap))\n            stepRange[1].push(numSteps)\n        } else {\n            stepRange[1].push(1)\n        }\n    }\n\n    return [stepRange, smoothRange]\n}\n\n// Default smoothing function from backend\nfunction meanAngle(smoothed: PointValue[], aspectRatio: number) {\n    let xRange = smoothed[smoothed.length - 1].lastStep - smoothed[0].lastStep\n    let yExtent = getExtent([smoothed], d => d.smoothed)\n    let yRange = yExtent[1] - yExtent[0]\n\n    if (xRange < 1e-9 || yRange < 1e-9) {\n        return 0\n    }\n\n    let angles = []\n    for (let i = 1; i < smoothed.length; i++) {\n        let dx = (smoothed[i].lastStep - smoothed[i - 1].lastStep) / xRange\n        let dy = (smoothed[i].smoothed - smoothed[i - 1].smoothed) / yRange\n        angles.push(Math.atan2(Math.abs(dy) * aspectRatio, Math.abs(dx)))\n    }\n\n    let angleSum = 0\n    for (let a of angles) {\n        angleSum += a\n    }\n    return angleSum / angles.length\n}\n\nexport function smooth45(series: PointValue[]): PointValue[] {\n    const MIN_SMOOTH_POINTS = 1\n    let fortyFive = Math.PI / 4\n    let hi = Math.max(1, series.length / MIN_SMOOTH_POINTS)\n    let lo = 1\n\n    let smoothed = smoothSeries(series, hi)\n\n    while (lo < hi) {\n        let m = (lo + hi) / 2\n        smoothed = smoothSeries(series, m)\n        let angle = meanAngle(smoothed, 0.5)\n        if (angle > fortyFive) {\n            lo = m + 1\n        } else {\n            hi = m\n        }\n    }\n\n    return smoothSeries(series, hi)\n}\n\nfunction getListFromBinary(binaryString: string): Float32Array {\n    let b64 = atob(binaryString)\n    const uint8Array = new Uint8Array(b64.length);\n    for (let i = 0; i < b64.length; i++) {\n      uint8Array[i] = b64.charCodeAt(i);\n    }\n    try {\n        let dataView = new DataView(uint8Array.buffer)\n        let floatArray = new Float32Array(dataView.byteLength / 4)\n        for (let i = 0; i < floatArray.length; i++) {\n            floatArray[i] = dataView.getFloat32(i * 4, true)\n        }\n        return floatArray\n    } catch (e) {\n        console.error(\"Error parsing binary data\", e)\n        return  new Float32Array(0);\n    }\n}",

url.includes('/auth/sign_up')) {\n                        setAppToken(token)\n                    } else {\n                        this.updateSession(token)\n                    }\n                }\n                if (xhr.status == 401 && retryAuth) {\n                    await this.getUser()\n                    try {\n                        let res = await this.sendHttpRequest(method, url, data, false)\n                        resolve(res)\n                    } catch (e) {\n                        reject(e)\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (xhr.status >= 400) {\n                    let errorMessage: string = null\n                    if (xhr.response != null) {\n                        if (xhr.response.hasOwnProperty('error')) {\n
